The lyrics are a puzzle, which is a bit difficult. You can guess it. I have always liked Chinese style dances. This time I covered the choreography of M Zi Ma Ma, and I couldn't help but sigh that the movements were too smooth. The song this time was actually changed at the last minute four days before the dance recording. After changing the song, I learned the dance again, picked out the movements, and bought the costumes. The time was very tight and I attached great importance to this manuscript. Unfortunately, there were still some minor problems on the scene. Originally, I prepared a cheongsam + Hanfu costume change. After recording, I found that the cheongsam effect was not very good, but for some reasons, the Hanfu version was only recorded with a mobile camera. Although there are some small regrets, the final effect is not bad. I hope you will like this video. Regardless of whether I can be selected for the Star Power this time, I am very grateful for your support and encouragement! Introduction Qixi Festival, also known as &quot;Chinese Valentine's Day&quot;, is the most romantic traditional festival. You will receive blessings and gifts that belong to your destiny. This year, there is a little love song as rich as milk tea called &quot;Want to Be With You&quot; that I hope you will sign for. His singer is &quot;Dong Xiangke&quot;, a newcomer from &quot;Produce Camp 2019&quot;. Like many newcomers who love singing, through competition after competition and training after training, they are gradually recognized by many people, including his mentor Su Youpeng. When Dong Xiangke released his first song &quot;Big Tree&quot;, he sang it himself Post on Weibo to recommend this powerful Vocal to everyone. A few months after his debut, he has released 3 new songs, from chasing dreams to flying against the wind to tenderness and sweetness. He constantly uses changing styles to outline his own musical surprises. Dong Xiangke sang a tender love song on Chinese Valentine's Day, an unforgettable little love song. In August, Chinese Valentine's Day brings a sweet breath; Confession is the time for romantic expression given by Chinese Valentine's Day. Many people who like Dong Xiangke are deeply impressed by his clean and ethereal voice. The love song style, unique voice, and sweet lyrics presented this time are as full of romance and aftertaste as this romantic festival, making people unable to help themselves. humming. The lyrics are concise and fresh, allowing people to wander in a very comfortable melody. The fresh and bright notes jump into the beautiful space between lovers. The sweet smell in the air is transformed into the most sincere expectation because of the repeated words &quot;I want to be with you&quot;. The song MV was released simultaneously, showing the most beautiful first love. The sweet and beautiful feeling in the MV, fresh and lovely style, is as eye-catching as any lover's first encounter. From the decoration layout, location of props to drinks, all colors are clean and warm. Since this MV is a love song, the director specially found a girl and Dong Xiangke to play a first love couple. Dong Xiangke, who is challenging the sweet style for the first time, is very shy and blushes even when looking at each other. There is a silly and cute charm in his shyness. With the pure visuals and Dong Xiangke's warm and sweet voice, the whole song makes people feel quite relieved. At present, the MV of this song is also online simultaneously with the song on Chinese Valentine's Day.
